 The survey was conducted on 24 and 25 November in 35 of Delhi's 70 assembly constituencies and the probability of error is about 4% (more or less)
 survey ke nateezon ke anusaar dilli main bijepi satta main waapas laut rahi he to congress ko bahut nuksaan hone ja rahaa he
 According to opinion poll, BJP will get 37 percent votes in Delhi, while Congress will get 29 percent votes
 keval 1 saal pehle raajnneeti ke akhaade main utarane vaali aam aadmi party (aap) ko 21 fisadi vot milane kaa anumaan he vahiin anya ko 13 fisadi vot milenge
 According to the estimates of the survey, BJP is going to gain 1 per cent votes while Congress will lose 11 per cent votes
 anya ko bhi 11 fisadi voton kaa nuksaan hoga

 Despite not having a single Muslim candidate, the BJP won 60 per cent of the seats under the influence of minorities
 bhagava lahar ne virodhiyon ke garh main aisa jowar paidaa kiya ki gandhi parivaar kii siton amethi or raibareli kii 10 main se chah seat bijepi ne kabja leen, jabaki mulaayam singh yadav ke garh itawa or mainpuri kii saat main se teen siten uski jholii main aa giriin
 Out of 105 seats Congress contested, it could win only 7, its worst performance since 1977
 uske ulat bijepi ke sahyogi apana dal ne jin 11 siton par ummidavaar khadey kiye the, unamem se 9 siten nikaal vah congress se aage ho gaya
 bjp's strategists were also filling their breath when the count of thorns came to a standstill
 403 main se kul 325 siten bijepi or uske sahyogiyon ke naam ho chuki thim
 This was the party's best performance in the state so far, ending its 14-year exile from Lucknow's power, while politically marginalizing regional parties like SP (47 seats) and BSP (19 seats)
 uttar pradesh main 2014 ke pradarshan ne yadi endie kii majboot neenv rakhi thi, to is baar ke vidhansabha chunaav main mili baari janadesh ne pradhanmantri modi ko unki agali chunauti yani 2019 ke loksabhaa chunaav ke paar jaakar sochane kaa adamya saahas diya he

 ve bole, ''aazaadee ke baad kii sabase badi vijay he, janata or modi ke netritv kii jeet he
 Modi has emerged as the most popular leader since independence
 "bijepi mukhyalay main 12 march ko modi ne bhi apane sambodhan main nae bharat ke liye shvijan 2022" kii ruparekha saamne rakhi
 This UP victory was not just a result of the atmosphere created in the election, but also a tremendous combination of Modi's growing popularity and Amit Shah's organizational skills despite two and a half years of rule at the Center
 yah jeet do saal kii yojanabaddh ranneeti, santhnik mashinari ko chaak-chauband karnaa or aakhir main ek shashakt prachaar kaa milajula nateeja he

 koi kushasan, gundgardee or bhrashtachar ko dhankane ke liye 100 kilometre kaa expresve banavaa kar janata ko murkh nahin bana saktaa
 "shah hopes that he will be able to take this wave outside UP as well
 bhaajapa adhyaksh shah ke bharose kii badi vajah brands modi he jo virodhiyon ko apni har chaal se chankane kaa madda rakhte hai or uskaa namoona dekh vipaksh vichlit ho uthta he

 twit tha—''modi bijepi se bade hai

 modi aadhunik bharat ke nae ram hai
 "the party won 221 seats out of 425 riding on the agenda of Kalyan Singh's staunch Hindutva in 1991 when it was promised to build a Ram temple in Ayodhya
 lekin uske baad ke chunaavon main party apana pradarshan kabhi aage kii ore nahin badha pai or 2012 main to vah apane sabase nichle str (47 seat) par pahunch gai
 But the BJP has changed its way of presenting its ideology
 is baar brands modi ko is tareeke se pesh kiya gaya jisane jati kii jang ko varg kii jang main badal daalaa or sushasan ke vaade ne majahabi card ko maat de di
 The Hindutva agenda of the BJP itself went backwards in some corner
 notebandi kaa mudda amir-garib kaa nayaa varg paidaa karne vaala sabit hua or modi ne apane sambodhano main lagaataar garibon kii baat kii
 The party's election slogan, "neither Gundaraj, nor corruption", was pasted behind 10,000 vehicles
 iske jariye bhaajapa ne sapa or basapa, donon par ek saath hamalaa bolaa tha

 There was also talk of putting the wandering criminals in jail
 modi ko ek aise maseehaa ke rup main dikhaaya gaya jo bhrashtachar or kaale dhan ke khilaaf abhiyaan kii aguai kar rahaa tha
 a poor-friendly Prime Minister who gave LPG to the poor under the Ujjwala scheme and opened accounts in banks under the Jan Dhan Yojana and arranged cheap loans for artisans and small entrepreneurs

 maury kehete hai, ''notebandi ne bijepi ke paksh main sataha ke neeche chal rahe samarthan ko lahar main tabdeel kar diya

 mayawati ne daliton or agadon kaa jo gathjod banaaya tha, usne bijepi ke savarna aadhaar main bhi send laga lee thi

 janvari kii baithak main hi unhone 40 binduon kaa ek agenda pradesh ke sanghathan mahasachiv sunil bansal ko saunpa or chunaav tak ise alag-alag bhaagon main baantkar amal karne kaa nirdesh diya

" " is mantra ke aadhaar par booth cametiyon kaa gathan shuru hua

 ise modi ne 1990 ke dashak main gujarat main viksit kiya tha

 boothon par hi bijepi ne 13

 In two torn Samajwadi Party, reconciliation efforts have intensified and Azam Khan has taken up the task
 donon hi khemon ne baatcheet ab sharton par aakar tik gai he
 On Tuesday, Mulayam and Akhilesh met for 4 hours, but the solution could not be found
 mulaayam ke ghar par akhilesh ke saath shivpal yadav bhi maujuud rahe, lekin teenon netaaon ne sulah par chuppi sadhi rakhi
 On Wednesday, there was a meeting at Mulayam Singh's house
 isamen shivpal yadav or ajam khan bhi shaamil hue
 Azam Khan went back from Mulayam's house after a long meeting
 ajam khan party main sulah kaa formula lekar saamne aae the
 Azam Khan has appealed to both sides to be a little lenient and to work together for the elections
 is baithak main naarad raay or omprakash samet kai netaa shaamil hue
 It is believed that Azam Khan will meet Akhilesh Yadav after this and discuss the possibilities ahead
 duusari odhkhilesh bhi apane samarthakonke saath baithak karenge or vivaad khatm karne ko lekar dobaaraa mulaayam se bhi mulaakaat kar sakate hai
 On reconciliation, Azam Khan said that Netaji is very positive and soft, he wants the dispute to end
 vivaad khatm karne ke liye jo kuch bhi karnaa pade, kar luungaa
 'azam' Formula 1 of Reconciliation
 mulaayam singh yadav rashtriya adhyaksh bane rahen,akhilesh apana daawa waapas le len
 2
 akhilesh ko pradesh adhyaksh kii kaman waapas de di jaae or tikat bantwaare main unki ahm bhoomika rahe
 3

 4
 mulaayam ke amar or akhilesh ke ramgopal ko party se baahar kaa rasta dikhaa diya jaae
 If reports are to be believed, Mulayam is now ready to put Amar Singh in charge of the party's international affairs, while Shivpal Yadav will leave Uttar Pradesh to look after national affairs
 vahiin akhilesh ummidavaaron ke bare main faisla karne ke liye swatantraaa di jaaegi
 Actually, on many occasions, the father-son is ready to accept the pairing, but according to experts, the powers with which the father and son are surrounded separately, somewhere they come to the forefront in a reconciliation
 mulaayam kii kamajori amar or shivpal hai, to vahiin akhilesh kaa haath ramgopal ke saath he
 After the father-son meeting in Lucknow, the Akhilesh faction met at Ram Gopal Yadav's house in Delhi and Ram Gopal Yadav also rejected all possibilities of reconciliation
 haalanki party ke saansad javed ali kaa kahana he ki party main koi jhagada nahin he or netaji hi unke adarsh hai
 Now Akhilesh's cycle: Naresh Agrawal: In a special conversation with the leader of Akhilesh faction Naresh Agarwal said that the cycle is now Akhilesh
 cycle samaajawaadee party kii he
 This two different bicycles reflect the two ideologies flowing in the country
 ek mehanatakash buzurg logon kii or duusari yuva shakti kii
 The thinking of youth cannot be avoided
 naye jamaane kii cycle ko bhi aage aana chahie
 The Election Commission will tell who rides the bicycle
 lekin samaajawaadee netaaon ke ghar main nai cycle ne jagah bana lee he
 Most of the mlas are with us: Ramgopal Yadav said after meeting the Election Commission on Tuesday that we have made our stand
 ramgopal yadav ne kaha ki hamaare saath party ke 90 fisadi vidhayak or 80 se 90 fisadi dailygats hai
 Therefore the real Samajwadi Party is the one whose president is Akhilesh Yadav
 isliye akhilesh yadav kii adhyakshata vaali party ko hi samaajawaadee party mana jaae
 Mulayam Singh Yadav, a source close to Mulayam's side in the Election Commission, has said that Mulayam's side is strong in the Election Commission, as calling sessions by members outside the party is unconstitutional
 sirf party adhyaksh hi adhiveshan bula saktaa he
 The decision to withdraw Akhilesh Yadav and Ram Gopal Yadav to the SP was not taken on any paper
 unka nishkasana waapas liya ja saktaa tha, lekin unhone adhiveshan bula liya
 Kiranmay Nanda made a new revelation, the old trustworthy Kiranmay Nanda, who was expelled from the Samajwadi Party by Mulayam Singh, has alleged that in two letters issued on January 1, the signature of Mulayam Singh Yadav is different
 is bayaan ke baad sin ko lekar nayaa vivaad shuru ho gaya he
 Significantly, on January 1, Akhilesh faction had held a session in Lucknow and announced to make Akhilesh Yadav as SP President
 iske baad mulaayam singh yadav ne is adhiveshan ko asanvaidhanik bataate hue do netaaon kiranmay nanda or naresh agarwal ko party se nikaalane kaa aadesh jari kiya tha or kaha tha ki sapa ke adhyaksh abhi mulaayam singh hi hai
